<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="revision-questions-teaching-and-learning-principles">Revision questions. Teaching and learning principles<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#revision-questions-teaching-and-learning-principles" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="1-kolb-s-definition-of-learning-is">1. Kolb's definition of learning is:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-kolb-s-definition-of-learning-is" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>a. Learning can be done through practice and experimentation.
b. Learning is the process whereby knowledge is created through the transformation of experience.
c. Learning is the process of acquisition of new knowledge.
d. Learning is an ongoing process.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="xx2-critical-thinking-is-very-important-for-nurses-because">XX2. Critical thinking is very important for nurses because:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#xx2-critical-thinking-is-very-important-for-nurses-because" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>a. Nursing process is always changing.
b. To make accurate and appropriate clinical decisions.
c. To plan and care for each unique client and client's problem.

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="question-25">QUESTION 25<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#question-25" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>in pedagogy knowledge is dependent on the learner while in andragogy learner depending on self.</li>
<li>in pedagogy learners and comes to the table with little life experience while in andragogy learners uses life experience as a foundation.</li>
<li>in pedagogy student advanced once they have completed the necessary steps while in andragogy learning is triggered by any number of life experience and not necessarily led by a designated instructor.</li>
<li>in pedagogy learning is prescribed by an instructor n sequence in a way that makes logical sense while in andragogy learning is prescribed by self.</li>
<li>in pedagogy learners are motivated by external source while in andragogy learners are motivated by increasing means, self-esteem, quality of life, problem solving, the quest for recognition.</li>
</ul>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="section-c-long-answer-answers">SECTION C: LONG ANSWER ANSWERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#section-c-long-answer-answers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="question29">QUESTION29<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#question29" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>[a]. Potentiated ingrideits of learning includes:</p>
<p>Motivation-A strong desire to learn wheter driven by intrinsic or extrinsic rewards and this encourages learners to engage in learning activities.</p>
<p>Active engagement-it requires active participation by engaging in activities like problem solving, discussion and hands on practice.</p>
<p>Practice -Regularly practicing helps to solidify knowledge and skills in long-term memory</p>
<p>Feedback -Receiving constructive feedback on performance helps learners to identify their strengths and weaknesses, make adjustments and improve.</p>
<p>[b]. Principles of adult learning :</p>
<p>Downloaded by Birosoft Enterprises (<a href="mailto:birosoftenterprises@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">birosoftenterprises@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<p>Active learning - Emphasize in participation and lerners involvement in learning process.</p>
<p>Integrated learning - Integrates of various parts in learning like basic sciences and clinical sciences leads to deeper understanding.</p>
<p>Concisistency in learning - Facilitator should prepare adequately to avoid contraindications and confusions as it can undermine learning.</p>
<p>Interests in learning - adults have personal interest to learn and this should be encouraged by motivating them with rewards.</p>
<p>Cumulative learning - This is how knowledge relates to the past experiences and it is useful in their future.</p>
<p>Learning for applications - this is how learners apply their knowledge and skills in problem solving discussions.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="question-30">QUESTION 30<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#question-30" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>[a]. Curriculum development approaches are:</p>
<ul>
<li>Learners-centered approach - Majorly used in primary and secondary schools to change the mindset of the learners.</li>
<li>Teacher-centered approach - The teacher becomes the main value of teaching and is the one who selects the teaching content and method to use in assessment.</li>
<li>Integrated approach - Integration in various activities in learning and teaching eg practical activities.</li>
<li>Subject-based approach - The subject lectures are the one determining the content to teach and the methods to use in teaching and how long it will take.</li>
<li>Competence based approach - majorly involves the practical aspect and professional competence and how teaching will be done in order to achieve the competency</li>
</ul>
<p>[b]. Factors influencing curriculum development :</p>
<ul>
<li>Academic factors - The research findings on effective teaching practices, learning outcomes and assessment methods may influence curriculum development. Also the knowledge, skills and experience of teachers can influence it.</li>
<li>Social factors - Curriculum should reflect the values, beliefs and traditions of the society it serves. It should address the needs of the community including issues like health.</li>
<li>Political factors - Curriculum development is influenced by government regulations and policies such as national standards or curriculum framework. Also government funding allocations can impact resource available for curriculum development and implementations.</li>
</ul>

<p>Economic factors-Curriculum can play a role in promoting economic growth and competitiveness.</p>
<p>Information and communication technology (ICT)-New technologies offer opportunities for innovative teaching methods and curriculum delivery eg online classes</p>
